           <a class="hidden-product-link" href="/collections/frontpage/products/cranberry-fresh" itemprop="url">
            BareSkinCare Acne Toner
           </a>
           <div class="info">
            <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="acne-cream,frontpage,chiral-skin-care-products" data-details-text="View full details" data-full-description="&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Need help with acne?&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;This toner is a wonderful solution for&lt;b&gt; oily and acne-prone skin !&lt;/b&gt; It contains glycolic acid polymer and salicylic acid in order to exfoliate and refine pores of congested skin. This ingredients soften the top layer of the epidermis, and the “cellular cement” that holds the corneum cells together will be resolved. It leaves the skin tight and smooth after use. The cranberry extract and witch hazel have &lt;b&gt;natural anti-bacterial and antiseptic benefits.&lt;/b&gt; Normal and mature skin may also enjoy this toner as a stimulating and clarifying alternative to the regular Bare Skin toner. Based on the skin’s needs, it can be used as a spot-treatment, or on the entire face.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;page&quot; title=&quot;Page 4&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;section&quot; style=&quot;background-color: rgb(100.000000%, 100.000000%, 100.000000%);&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;layoutArea&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;column&quot;&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;This toner was specially formulated for oily and acne-prone skin. It contains glycolic acid polymer and salicylic acid for refining PORES and keeping congested skin mildly exfoliated. The cranberry extract and witch hazel have natural antibacterial and antiseptic benefits. Normal and mature skins... &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;SKIN CONDITION(S): &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;Acne prone skin conditions &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;BENEFITS: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;CRANBERRY FRESH is contains both Glycolic Acid Polymer and Salicylic Acid which both soften keratinized barrier cells, as well as dissolve the top layer of corneum cells and the 'cellular cement' that holds the corneum cells together. This leaves the skin feeling smooth and tight after use. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;FOCUS INGREDIENTS:&lt;br&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;• &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Witch Hazel Extract &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;– antiseptic, increases circulation&lt;br&gt; • &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Glycolic Acid Polymer &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;– exfoliating, smoothing&lt;br&gt; • &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Salicylic Acid &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;– keratolytic&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;DIRECTIONS FOR USE: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;Use once or twice daily after cleansing. Apply to cotton pad and wipe skin gently. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;INGREDIENTS: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;(Aqua) Distilled Water, Witch Hazel (Hamamelis Virginiana) Extract, Ethyl Alcohol, Glycolic Acid Polymer, Salicylic Acid, L-castor Oil Methyl Glycol. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;CAUTION: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;For external use only. Avoid contact with eyes. Keep out of reach of children. Test for sensitivity&lt;br&gt; – discontinue or reduce usage if irritating to skin. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;SUNBURN ALERT:&lt;br&gt; This product contains an alpha hydroxy acid (AHA) that may increase your skin’s sensitivityto the sun and particularly the possibility of sunburn. Use a sunscreen and limit sunexposure while using this product and for a week afterwards. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

CLEANSER maintains the moisture level with the presence of Shea Butter. The Yucca Saponins Extract is an anti-irritant and increases cell growth. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;FOCUS INGREDIENTS:&lt;br&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;• &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Shea Butter&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;: moisturizing&lt;br&gt; • &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Yucca Saponins Extract: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;cleansing, anti-irritant • &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Flower Petal Oils&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;: ChiromatherapyTM &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Heidi Fogelsong, Media Personality for Bare Skin&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;A wonderful cleanser for all skin types ! Whether you have dry, oily, normal, mature, or acne skin This cleanser will assist to balance your skin, while thoroughly removing dirt and makeup without dryness or residue. It lathers strongly, and you only need a tiny amount. It leaves your skin clean without stripping it of all natural oils. It is a fragrant combination of calendula, chamomile, rosemary, sage, passionflower, papaya and raspberry extracts. With presence of Shea Butter, and Aloe Vera, it maintains the skin’s moisture level while controlling oiliness. The Yucca Saponins extract is an anti-irritant and increases the skin’s cell growth.&lt;/p&gt;

           <div class="info">
            <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="frontpage,chiral-skin-care-products,oily-skin,oily-skin-1" data-details-text="View full details" data-full-description="&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;NEW BARE SKIN CARE PRODUCT&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;

&lt;p&gt;Our NEW ENHANCER has been updated and improved. This &lt;strong&gt;elegan&lt;/strong&gt;t AHA has increased to 10% glycolic acid.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The key to regaining or maintaining youthful skin is exfoliation! The Bare Skin Care Enhancer is a highly effective lotion that acts as an exfoliant to polish and refine damaged skin. It smoothes fine lines and imperfections, controls excess oiliness, and helps eliminate discolorations. While it moisturizes surface layer of the skin, it gently exfoliates to create smoother and suppler skin.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;There are several ingredients in the &lt;strong&gt;New Bare Skin Enhancer&lt;/strong&gt; that gives it the muscles needed to strengthen skin.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The first ingredient is Glycolic Acid, a beloved Alpha Hydroxy Acid (AHA) used as an exfoliant to remove dead skin cells and smooth skin texture. It also effortlessly &lt;strong&gt;reduces signs of fine lines and wrinkles. &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The second ingredient is &lt;strong&gt;Hydrolyzed Collagen, the main structural protein found in skin&lt;/strong&gt;. This is added to supplement the already-present supply created naturally by the body, &lt;strong&gt;plumping skin and leaving it feeling full and taut&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The third strengthening ingredient is Glucosamine HCI, which &lt;strong&gt;improves moisture content in the skin, hydrating it&lt;/strong&gt; properly for the long term. It also &lt;strong&gt;strengthens connective tissues to resist breakdown, combat environmental toxins, and to secure protection.&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;Once the skin is protected, it’s time to calm and heal the skin... there are &lt;strong&gt;three soothing ingredients&lt;/strong&gt; contribute to this process.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The first is Olea Europaea Fruit Oil, more commonly known as &lt;strong&gt;Olive Oil&lt;/strong&gt;, which is&lt;strong&gt; rich in vitamin E and antioxidants&lt;/strong&gt;. It also &lt;strong&gt;replaces skin moisture, restores elasticity, and acts as an anti‐inflammatory and anti‐bacterial agent&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The second ingredient is Tocopherol, a naturally occurring fat-soluble form of &lt;strong&gt;vitamin E.&lt;/strong&gt; It also acts as an &lt;strong&gt;antioxidant and anti-inflammatory,&lt;/strong&gt; and protects skin from oxidative stress.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The third is Allantoin, which possesses &lt;strong&gt;soothing, moisturizing and skin softening properties while promoting healing and healthy cell renewal.&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The lack of wrinkles on faces of our employees and Bare Skin Care customers, without the help of injections, is unique to the world. &lt;strong&gt;How unique is your skin?&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Works great on bareskin.&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

          <div class="thumbnail-overlay">
           <a class="hidden-product-link" href="/collections/frontpage/products/bare-skin-care-moisturizer" itemprop="url">
            BareSkinCare Moisturizer
           </a>
           <div class="info">
            <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="frontpage,chiral-skin-care-products,cleanser-toner-moisturizer" data-details-text="View full details" data-full-description="&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Best Moisturizer 2017&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;State of the art moisturizer&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Contains collagen&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Tired of dry skin?&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Bare Skin Care Moisturizer is a wonderfully light yet highly effective cream. It contains a combination of all&lt;b&gt; state-of-the art moisturizing ingredients&lt;/b&gt; the skin needs to restore deep cellular hydration, plumpness and fullness. It is never heavy and greasy, yet provides rich moisture to dry skin by penetrating several levels of Hyaluronic Acid deep into the epidermal skin layers. It also greatly assists the skin’s need for additional hydration, while going through an intense skin repair process where cell turnover and exfoliation might lead to temporary dryness. It &lt;b&gt;contains collagen &lt;/b&gt;which supports firmness and plumpness of skin. Beta Fructan retains hydration in the skin cells, and Beta Glucosamine strengthens the skin. A wonderful addition to the Bare Skin Care Anti-Aging Serum and/or the Bare Skin Care Natural Young C Serum when the skin needs an additional relief from dryness. Wonderful also for eye and neck area.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;page&quot; title=&quot;Page 7&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;section&quot; style=&quot;background-color: rgb(100.000000%, 100.000000%, 100.000000%);&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;layoutArea&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;column&quot;&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(0.000000%, 0.000000%, 100.000000%);&quot;&gt;DESCRIPTION: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;White Cream which softens skin, leaving a smooth, silky feeling, and contains natural moisturizers and collagen to firm the skin. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;SKIN CONDITION(S): &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;All, Anti-Age &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(0.000000%, 0.000000%, 100.000000%);&quot;&gt;BENEFITS: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 14.000000pt; font-family: 'Times';&quot;&gt;Light, non-comedogenic moisturizer softens dry skin and leaves a smooth, silky feeling. Contains natural moisturizers and collagen for firming. For all skin types. Use anytime the skin feels dry. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;FOCUS INGREDIENTS:&lt;br&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;• &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Fructooligosaccharides &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;- D-beta-Glucosamine is one of the many small molecular weight chemicals that make the natural moisturizing factor (NMF). Macroscopically, D-beta-Glucosamine applied topically alleviates skin dryness, facilitates exfoliation, with smoothness replacing “scales”. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;• &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Sodium PCA – &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;stable enzyme that converts the destructive superoxide radical into a less dangerous form, hydrogen peroxide &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;DIRECTIONS FOR USE: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;Use once daily or when necessary. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;INGREDIENTS: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;Aqua (Water), Caprylic/Capric Triglyceride, Cetearyl Glucoside, Cetearyl Alcohol,&lt;br&gt; Coco- Caprylate / Caprate, Glycerin, Glyceryl Stearate, Glycol Distearate, Sodium PCA, Fructooligosaccharides (D-beta), Hydrolyzed Collagen, Polysorbate 60, Palmitic Acid, Stearic Acid, Myristic Acid, Dimethicone, Cetyl Alcohol, Xanthan Gum, Benzyl Alcohol, Propylene Glycol, Diazolidinyl Urea, Methylparaben, Propylparaben &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;ul&gt;

&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;img src="//cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0160/2294/files/bs_pic25_large.jpg?v=1485806061" alt=""&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/li&gt;

&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Want to even your skin tone? Get rid of ugly brown spots with Perfect Tone Serum.&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Perfect Tone Serum provides additional support to &lt;b&gt;even skin tone&lt;/b&gt; and &lt;b&gt;correct discoloration&lt;/b&gt;. Ingredients are a combination of 2% Hydroquinone and &lt;b&gt;natural skin brighteners&lt;/b&gt; delivered to the skin in serum form. Based on different skin types, different length of product use is suggested, it is therefore important that a skin care professional consults with you on the proper use of this product. Sun exposure should be limited by using a sunscreen agent or protective clothing when using or after using this product, in order to prevent darkening from reoccurring. This product is more effective if used with Bare Skin Care Rejuvenation Serum, which helps to turn the skin over and more rapidly and effectively eliminating brown or age spots (hyperpigmentation). &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;PERFECT TONE is a highly effective, gentle, lightening product, available with hydroquinone.  Hydroquinone is the key ingredient.  Kojic Acid and Azelaic Acid are supported by a low dose of L-lactic Acid to exfoliate dead skin cells on the surface of the skin, allowing the lightening ingredients to penetrate more effectively.  Licorice Root Extract has a de-pigmenting (natural lightener) effect as well as an inhibitory effect on melanin synthesis due to its ability to act as a tyrosinase inhibitor.  This formula with Hydroquinone supplies an additional bleaching boost for those skins that are not sensitive to Hydroquinone. &lt;/p&gt;

           <div class="info">
            <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="anti-aging-product,frontpage,chiral-skin-care-products" data-details-text="View full details" data-full-description="&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Benefits&lt;br&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;

&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Younger firmer skin&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/li&gt;

&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Look 10 years younger! Rejuvenate your face with Bare Skin. &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;page&quot; title=&quot;Page 11&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;section&quot; style=&quot;background-color: rgb(100.000000%, 100.000000%, 100.000000%);&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;layoutArea&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;column&quot;&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;DESCRIPTION: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;This serum is specially designed by Dr. Bollmann as a strong Retinol solution to replace Retin-A. It is less irritating than Retin-A but as effective. It contains other ingredients that increase its effectiveness, including glycolic acid polymer complex. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;SKIN CONDITION(S): &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;All skin conditions &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;BENEFITS: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;REJUVENATION SERUM is an AHA form of 'complexed' Retinol (Vitamin A) together with Glycolic Acid to create an energized and synergized complex. This complex takes advantage of the physical and chemical forces that bind Glycolic Acid to Retinol (Vitamin A). Therefore, the complex synergy will give you much better results than each ingredient used alone. The REJUVENATION SERUM coaxes the skin to re-select its epidermal building blocks and therefore, the wrinkles that sustain &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;adult keratins will slowly give way to the smoother, more elastic and wrinkle resistant fetal-type keratins. Retinol is a skin renewing vitamin which is essential for tissue growth. Glycolic Acid Polymer is more natural to the skin, and helps to strengthen collagen and elastin. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;FOCUS INGREDIENTS:&lt;br&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;• &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Witch Hazel Extract &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;– antiseptic, increases circulation&lt;br&gt; • &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;D-beta-fructan &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;– retains moisture&lt;br&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;• D-beta-glucosamine &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;– strengthening&lt;br&gt; • &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Retinol/Glycolic Acid Polymer Complex &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;– exfoliating, smoothing • &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Tangerine Essential Oil &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;- chiromatherapyTM &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;DIRECTIONS FOR USE: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;Use once or twice daily on clean skin as part of the Bare Skin program or under a moisturizer. TITRATE AS NECESSARY AS THIS IS A STRONG PRODUCT. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;page&quot; title=&quot;Page 11&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;section&quot; style=&quot;background-color: rgb(100.000000%, 100.000000%, 100.000000%);&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;layoutArea&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;column&quot;&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;INGREDIENTS: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;Aqua (Distilled Water, Witch Hazel (Hamamelis Virginiana) Extract, Propylene Glycol, Vitamin A Palmitate, Retinol/Glycolic Acid Polymer Complex, D-beta-fructan, D-beta- glucosamine, Xanthan Gum, Carmine, Tangerine (Citrus Reticulata) Oil &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;CAUTION: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'ArialMT';&quot;&gt;For external use only. Avoid contact with eyes. Keep out of reach of children. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;p&gt;A fantastic serum for skin that needs wrinkle reduction, cell turnover, skin renewal and correction! This serum is a complex synergy of Retinol (Vitamin A) and Glycolic Acid. Retinol is a skin-renewing vitamin which is essential for tissue growth. Glycolic Acid Polymer further assists cell turnover and strengthens collagen and elastin. The complex synergy of these ingredients contained in this serum, gives you much better results than each ingredient used alone. This serum triggers a process in the skin that re-selects its epidermal building blocks, and therefore lines and wrinkles will slowly give way to smoother, more elastic and wrinkle resistant skin. The serum is very powerful and as cell turnover starts, some flaking may occur. Go slow with the serum, if your skin is sensitive, and let the skin renewal process take place gradually.&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12.000000pt; font-family: 'Arial'; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;DESCRIPTION: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

It prepares the skin for the penetration of other products. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

It acts like a key to unlock the cell membrane. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

       <h2 class="title">
        Skin Care Programs
       </h2>
      </a>
      <div class="feature_divider">
      </div>
      <div class="section clearfix">
       <p>
        While all Bare Skin Care products can be used individually, best results are obtained by using the full program for the indicated problem -
        <strong>
         <a href="https://bareskincare.com/collections/skin-care-programs/products/program-for-wrinkles" title="Program for Wrinkles">
          WRINKLES
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="https://bareskincare.com/collections/skin-care-programs/products/program-for-wrinkles" title="Program for Sun Damage">
          SUN DAMAGE
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="https://bareskincare.com/collections/skin-care-programs/products/bare-skin-care-program-for-hyperpigmentation" title="Program for Hyperpigmentation">
          HYPERPIGMENTATION
         </a>
        </strong>
        (pigment problems - melasma),
        <strong>
         <a href="https://bareskincare.com/collections/skin-care-programs/products/bare-skin-care-program-for-hyperpigmentation" title="Skin Lightening">
          SKIN LIGHTENING
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="https://bareskincare.com/collections/skin-care-programs/products/bare-skin-care-program-for-acne-1" title="Program for Acne">
          ACNE
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="https://bareskincare.com/collections/skin-care-programs/products/program-for-oily-skin" title="Program for Oily Skin ">
          OILY SKIN
         </a>
        </strong>
        , or scars. Our
        <a href="https://bareskincare.com/collections/skin-care-programs/products/bare-skin-care-basic-program" title="Program for Skin Health">
         <strong>
          BASIC PROGRAM
         </strong>
        </a>
        is for skin health - restoring, correcting, protecting and maintaining the health of YOUR skin.
       </p>
       <p>
        Accelerate your beauty skin care program with these advanced Anti-Aging Skin Care Programs. Remove wrinkles, fix aging skin, sun damaged skin, and discolorations in skin tone.
